#√±√¢√•√™√∞√Æ√¢√º/√≤¬∏√π√† √¢ √ß√†√¢√®√±√®√¨√Æ√±√≤√® √Æ√≤ √Ø√Æ√´√† √®√£√∞√Æ√™√† (√¢√ª√ß√ª√¢√†√•√≤√±√ø √∑√•√∞√•√ß [Player.])
defined_text = {
	name = GetMotherInLaw

	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			is_female = yes
		}
		localisation_key = GetRelation_MotherOfHusband
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			is_female = no
		}
		localisation_key = GetRelation_MotherOfWife
	}
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = GetMotherInLaw_FB
	}
}

	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = __ #alt_culture_china_postfix
	text = {
		trigger = {
			non_historical_culture_names_in_alt_start_trigger = yes
			NOT = { han = { has_flag = is_name_randomized_flag } }
			offmap_china = {
				offmap_ruler = {
					dynasty_head = {
						culture = han
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localisation_key = AYA_CULTURE_UNPOSTFIX
	}
